src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSDHpicDdl0ZRkqWTHLe85z2K2Z5Oyybo6DdzMibyNRz6wxmvTxYYsmlXA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">穷则思变是亘古不变的道理，自己饭都吃不饱哪还管什么公序良俗。而且没受过教育的年轻人们并不会将自己的不顺归咎于上层政治家和寡头，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">而是认为涌入俄罗斯的外族人抢夺了他们的财富，</span>挤轧了他们原有的生存空间。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这时极右翼思想就在俄罗斯有了市场，除了光头党之外，俄罗斯民族团结党、雅利安兄弟会等<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">白人至上组织</span>也在全俄范围内遍地开花。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">1990年代涌现出的极右翼激进亚文化</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">背后是苏联邦解体前混乱的社会状态和疲乏的经济</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：https://www.liveinternet.ru）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(226, 224, 224);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-w=\"576\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUS12zaCqBDDW2vnYP5O5oiaRkDvXjyQLcFa8eZDAx5AoE0YgwXOhRAejg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这其中的一些组织<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">公开承认自己是“新纳粹分子”，</span>比如光头党就视阿道夫·希特勒为精神导师，尽管斯拉夫人也是希特勒计划中被奴役的种族，但是他“教会了白人如何维护自己的民族身份”。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">虽然希特勒要维护的白人中并不包括他们</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">但对于现状的不满试图通过激进的思想和行为来发泄</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">纵观近现代史，激进人群的最优代表非希特勒莫属了</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：https://www.liveinternet.ru）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-w=\"747\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUS4kXQOyOPKkDojLzEPticsg0a4MFFsNrOOpia37gEfPDcoGEHXE9kea4w/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);text-align: center;font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">鞑靼恐惧症</p></section><section style=\"margin: 8px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(189, 112, 112);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">俄罗斯的新纳粹和种族主义者与过去的纳粹分子有相似之处，比如都鼓吹白人种族优越论，都仇视犹太人等外族等等，但他们之前的<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">差异还是大于共性。</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">将纳粹主义与俄罗斯本土文化相结合的布尔什维克党</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">指导思想就是“俄罗斯就是一切，其余什么都不是”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">走的也是极权主义和法西斯主义的路子</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Wikipedia）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(226, 224, 224);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.7899761\" data-w=\"419\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSD8USicGBt5Yf85qwEia6kMY3ibaqh4SMvnp3rptMVWHugGibIRPrsydg8A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">俄罗斯新纳粹<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">对斯拉夫以外的民族都怀有敌视态度，</span>甚至包括西欧、北美和西亚的白人。在他们眼里属于不同国家的乌克兰人、白罗斯人、塞尔维亚人等归于斯拉夫大类的民族都可以是自己人，但本国的非斯拉夫民族则是异类。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;\">他们的暴力行动主要</span>针对的是国内的北高加索各民族和来自中亚前加盟共和国<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">信奉伊斯兰教的少数民族。</span>这些人基本符合俄族对于“鞑靼人”的认知。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">欧洲人所说的“鞑靼人”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">广义上是指俄国境内使用突厥语各族的统称</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">即使他们不喜欢，也无法阻挡政府合并克里米亚</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">克里米亚的突厥人可是“纯正鞑靼”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（阿塞拜疆人以及北高加索、中亚、伏尔加河流域突厥语各族）</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：https://zen.yandex.com）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(226, 224, 224);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-w=\"424\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSRJErbZc68OwsnCRjTMxzc4hia7Hk62xuICibJFKK1RqqeFExEcATDAuA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">对这些人的憎恨在俄语中有个专有名词叫“鞑靼恐惧症”，最早来源于金帐汗国时期蒙古人对当地斯拉夫人的残酷统治，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">进而延伸到一切游牧民族和穆斯林的仇视。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">鞑靼恐惧症有两个表现形式，它们分别来源于两个在俄罗斯人之间流传的经久不衰的言论。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">一是惧怕有鞑靼血统的人与俄族人通婚，他们认为通婚后代会沾染到黄种人野蛮和低智商的基因。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">二是苏联解体之后<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">俄罗斯民族人口逐渐减少，</span>而来自于中亚和高加索地区的少数民族和穆斯林人口则在不断增加。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">莫斯科大清真寺也被称为“鞑靼清真寺”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">原建筑以不合理的原因被拆除了</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">不过</span><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">很快又建造了新的建筑来弥补</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（2015年，普京和埃尔多安参加大教堂清真寺落成典礼）</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：克里姆林宫）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-w=\"790\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSNSLuTqKAOzmDjp0xj9Av2cyKzvZmWtS0AZbBLhEKibhOH35qniaicVOfg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">有些极右翼组织趁机<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">大肆宣传“人口替换论”，</span>称如果现在不将这些人赶走，那么未来的俄罗斯将被这些异族、异端和异教徒占据。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">上世纪90年代的<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">车臣战争</span>加剧了这种仇恨情绪。其实在沙俄时期车臣人与俄族就结下了血海深仇，二战期间车臣和克里米亚鞑靼人曾一道投靠德国反苏，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">被苏联视为背叛行为遭到打压和流放。</span>苏联解体之后双方的摩擦逐渐失控升级，最终酿成2次车臣战争。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">两次车臣战争，俄罗斯一败一胜<br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">那57个万人冢是伴随着无数俄罗斯家庭和车臣人的悲惨记忆</p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Natalia Medvedeva / Wikipedia）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(226, 224, 224);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-w=\"524\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSgs2ICNXedREfGyvxicrHqSok0vdZ5ic7gCMyxIbRstQrm0g5FOVwtazA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">俄罗斯军队在车臣战争中的表现并不好，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">付出了惨重的代价却没能达到目标。</span>对于很多俄族人来说，他们的兄弟、父亲死在了战场上异族人的手里，而他们生活在这一地区的族人却被迫离开家园。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">俄罗斯以死亡近4000人的战绩赢得了战争</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">但却不能让车臣人真正的归顺</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（车臣战争中阵亡的俄罗斯士兵）</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Svm-1977 / wikipedia）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1\" data-w=\"819\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSr45mr0tpnUUx4VMxoQZunkhjwEZ0b5qYy1ib2P3IB33HJBkOAFFtyzw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这种挫败感加剧了俄罗斯社会上对高加索地区民族和中亚面孔的恐惧和愤怒，<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">敌对情绪从战场上弥漫到了整个社会。</span>如果说受过教育有良好修养，或者接受过苏联时期民族团结教育的人们尚且能够保持克制，思考一下问题的根源，没上过几天学的年轻混混们可就直接多了。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">一旦找到“同道中人”，这种冲动就会持续发酵</span></p><p 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">生活不如意</span>的时候。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">不再有全民免费医疗，</span>很多俄罗斯家庭负担不起正规的医疗费用；另一方面则是因为<span style=\"color: rgb(189, 112, 112);box-sizing: border-box;\">社会淹没在了酒精中</span>——颓废失望的情绪弥漫，时代的变化让人们对未来感到迷茫，于是年迈而疲惫的中老年男人选择逃避，借酒消愁，最终伤害了身体。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">公元13世纪，蒙元军队用战争的手段征服了亚洲大陆的大部分文明。大元皇帝忽必烈对此似乎并不满足，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">他还想将自己的权势扩张到更远的地方。</span></p></section></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">蒙古大军在陆上所向披靡</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">没征服的地方都是太冷太热太远，以及隔海相望▼</span></p></section></section><section style=\"margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">灭掉南宋之后，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">蒙元帝国组成了一支由高丽人和南宋降将为主的水师，浩浩荡荡地向日本列岛进发了。</span>在忽必烈的想象之中，十万大军必定能以摧枯拉朽之势吞噬那个东海以东的日出之国。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">然而元军的第一波攻势并不顺利，指挥官<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">不适应日本山地地形的作战套路</span>，元军被暂时赶回了船上，筹备第二次进攻。</p></section></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">蒙元进军日本</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">战斗集中在朝鲜海峡上的对马岛和北九州</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">如同征讨爪哇国一样</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">两次战斗以失败告终，而海上因素是致败关键</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span></p></section></section><section style=\"margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: data-ratio=\"1.2731481\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" style=\"margin: 0px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">就在这时，一<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">场持续两天的剧烈台风袭击并摧毁了大部分元军舰船，彻底改变了这场战争的进程，</span>元军战败主帅范文虎逃回中国。日本神道教僧人将这场台风称为“神风”，这也是二战期间神风敢死队的来源。</p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这个改变了日本国运的历史故事背后，是风的强大能量对人类社会从未停歇的改变。</p></section></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">第二次元日战争中元朝军队的失败并非只是军事战术上的原因，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">元军将登陆日本的时间和地点选择在农历7月，北纬34°的壹岐岛上。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这是一个致命的失误，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">因为那时那地出现台风的概率很大。</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">夏天正是西太平洋台风最活跃的时候</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">比如今年8月下旬的台风“巴威”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">就一路北上甚至在朝鲜登陆</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：wikipedia@NASA）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(223, 223, 223);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.3333333\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSDdkDQsabJibZfgpVscemzbfWiaNlCnkGcZK2WoQ1WyElhaCUHVINVk4A/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">我们知道风的本质是空气的流动，而空气的运动并非变幻莫测而是有迹可循的。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">空气<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">也遵循着热胀冷缩的自然规律。</span>地球表面的热量主要来源于太阳光的照射，而陆地和水面在太阳照射下的升温和降温有所不同，一般情况下陆地在白天升温更快，在夜晚降温更快。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">上过中学物理课的同学肯定都知道</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">不同物质的比热容差异巨大，比如二氧化硅和水</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">所以同样的热量，沙漠可以更快升温</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">并带动沙漠上方的空气更快升温</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Merkushev Vasiliy / shutterstock）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 2px;border-style: none;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(167, 167, 167);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.9898148\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSBs3NpRVicj2JBkgzQrs1DUlzRwLfxryYlpb7ibgSjKLLTu1MCORDdQWA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">这就导致了所谓“海陆热力性质差异”，</span>在夏季日光强烈的时候，陆地上空的空气总是会受热膨胀，单位空间的空气密度小于海洋上空；到了冬季，海洋能蕴藏更多的热量，导致海陆气压呈现出与夏季完全相反的态势。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">15年来平均海平面压力</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">上图是6-8月（夏季），高压集中在海上</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">下边是12-2月（冬季），高压集中在陆上（尤其亚洲）</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: Connolleyt / Wikipedia）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.0337423\" data-w=\"652\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSrKOextZ6TicK2DdzW4KokAW1WFVJa6kUThgqE0OVQ3GJ15jvNuHn8JA/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">空气密度小意味着气压低，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">空气由高气压地区向低气压地区流动，</span>这种现象被称之为“风”。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">而由于海陆热力性质差异，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">在大陆和海洋之间大范围的、风向随季节有规律改变的风，被称为“季风”。</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">季风气候区一般也分布在大陆上相对靠近海洋的部分</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">“海陆热力性质差异”越强烈，季风也就越强烈</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">东亚位于世界上最大的大陆——亚欧大陆和世界上最大的海洋——太平洋的中间地带，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">是世界上最典型的季风气候区。</span>季风影响了东亚的方方面面，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">分明的四季、严格的节气、雨热同期降水规律等等特点塑造了东亚民族的生产方式和民族性格。</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">夏季的时候，西北太平洋的副热带高压区是东亚夏季季风的策源地，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">它的存在直接控制和影响着太平洋上生成的一个又一个台风。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">每年夏天高压区都会随着太阳直射点的北移而向北移动，给我国华北、东北地区带来大范围的降水。而元军登陆日本所在的壹岐岛约在北纬34°，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: border-box;\">但不知道原理并不妨碍那些了解了风能状况的人去尝试利用这种能量。</span>早在两千多年前，中国人就发明了风车这一精妙的机械，将看不见摸不着的风能化为机械能。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">风车的使用大大解放了人力，中国人用风车来冶炼金属、提水浇田，利用风这一随处可见的强大能量改善生活质量。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;color: rgb(55, 144, 163);font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">百年能源革命的挑战者</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 8px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(110, 141, 156);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">其实，再往远处推，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">对于风能的利用始于人类对大海的征服欲望。</span>一个标志性的事件就是帆的出现，它让人类可以利用风的力量穿越大面积的水域，不再望洋兴叹。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">帆是水上运输的关键发明</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">从河、湖开始，到内海再到大洋</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">没有帆，人类不可能把船划到世界尽头</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（尼罗河上小帆船，阿斯旺附近）</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：shutterstock@leshiy985）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.9833333\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUStf56pUoHibhVn0wclAwzOFcBJeGLuXpRXgMqYW94me2vkqrVVaQW5PA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">目前确定最早的帆船来自于古埃及，继而被地中海沿岸的海洋文明发扬光大，从带着固定风帆的舢板发展成为大航海时代乘风破浪的巨舰，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">推动了工业文明时代的到来。</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">地中海其实是相对风平浪静的海域</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">在地中海航行尚可以桨、帆并用</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这里也因此成为早期航海技术发展的“温室”</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">成为之后大航海时代的起点▼</span></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(223, 223, 223);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.0888889\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUS6whw04VZic6dxbcX6lM0BnJ52tS0FD3rja5Ul4UKGlFE6FrLRm3hKdg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">然而风帆成就了航海时代和科技大发展，但也因此面临淘汰的命运。由于第一次工业革命带来的蒸汽机让化石能源可以以一种效率更高和更稳定的方式为人所利用，对风能的开发也陷入了一个漫长的停滞期。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">相比帆船，轮船既不靠风力也不靠人力</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">靠自己就可以滚滚向前、行动自如</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这在古代文明看来简直难以置信</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：shutterstock@Marzolino）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 1px;border-style: solid;border-radius: 0px;border-color: rgb(223, 223, 223);box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.0231481\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSYBA1audVEXggZeTuhAeibjOqoKKiac8bKh4WS8fDt8xsOy9gblzHg2Nw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">内燃机、火力发电等技术的成熟使得风能被边缘化，煤炭和石油从全世界发掘出来被运送到工厂，为城市的运转提供能量。但在城市以外的地方，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">有一个人默默钻研着风能如何以一种更好的方式为人类所利用。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">1887年，安德森学院的教授詹姆斯·布莱斯居住在在苏格兰东北部阿伯丁郡下面一个小村庄的花园别墅之中，苦于无法利用城市电力并致力于研究风力发电可能性的他购买了一个市面上刚出现的酸铅电池，在自家花园里建造了一个风车利用风力为电池供电，点亮了院子里的灯。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这个庞然大物</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">叶轮直径是17米，叶片由144个雪松木制成</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：</span>梅塞利<span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">/</span>Wikipedia<span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">）</span></span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.035014\" data-w=\"714\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSMThX4KkSFyCmmPrTTILNDWIkxT3icPfNlJaHBop1AQ0uWKxu5LsicHGA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这是人类历史上第一台自动风力发电机，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">自此用清洁能源替代化石能源点亮城市、为工业发展提供动力成为了可能。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">风电对比代表旧模式的火电有着自身独特的优势，</span>首先风能分布非常广泛，全世界各地都能获取到。其次只要太阳保持稳定输出，风能几乎没有耗尽的那一天。而且风能足够环保，转化过程中极少排出有害污染物，在环境问题日益严重的今天有着现实意义。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">而且在那些相对偏远的沿海地区</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">风能这种可以相对稳定的自给自足能源</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">能解决当地供电难的问题</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：Ana del Castillo / Shutterstock）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.9907407\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSfJlric8PunOuFIYY6NTQ1fzKAKPnBVXyrZxZQ2soibyuV8FvyuPEZPPg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">风力发电对于国人来说已经不是陌生事物，但仍然有很多人不知道，自1986年中国的第一座并网风电机组在山东建成以来。<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">我国已经是全球风电装机总量最大、海上风电装机总量第三的国家，是名副其实的风电大国。</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">草原上那么大的风，不用真的可惜了</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（内蒙古辉腾锡勒草原风电）</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：戈文 / Tuchong Genius）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.9824074\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSuZyib8YXSQdPKquAtVwX0SiahOXARkGTlFISicvibtuPLlYeMCj8suYBsg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">今天我国西北、华北和东南沿海均被视为风力资源丰富的地区，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">这种清洁能源很快在能源紧张的我国展现出了巨大的潜力，获得了政府和企业的重视。</span>随着2006年《可再生能源法》的颁布，风电产业正式走上快车道，发展到今天，中国已经有了高达超过21005万千瓦的风电累计装机量，远高于第二名美国，占到了世界总装机量的1/3左右。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：</span>giusparta /  Adobe Stock / 图虫创意<span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">）</span></span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.9657407\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSMTjSjPTSxRDcl05lEsAedvOD0qaibib3cwbMvO3855ibNl997ewtjB4SQ/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">从东南沿海到伊犁河谷，从南海之滨到内蒙古草原，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">风电作为国家电网的一部分正在我国发挥着自己的作用，也启迪着世界能源变革的道路，</span>风也许就是未来。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section><section style=\"text-align: center;color: rgb(55, 144, 163);font-size: 17px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"> </p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">先乘风才能破浪</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 8px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 0.8;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 0.8em solid rgb(110, 141, 156);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 0;\"><section style=\"line-height: 0;width: 0px;\"><svg viewbox=\"0 0 1 1\" style=\"vertical-align:top;\"></svg></section></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">物理意义上的风确有独特的能量属性。古人也早已认可了这种雄壮的自然现象的价值，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">人类甚至把风认为是构成大自然最基本的元素，</span>《周易》中八卦中的巽卦所代表的意象就是风。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">风的特点是你看不见它，但却能感受到它的力量。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">春风吹又生</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：topphoto / 图虫创意）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.7712963\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSXWNfEoiayYiaIKKykM2gYExP90Iibg1ibzvPlDERpUf5VgJx1ibYFLSrwUg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">这种力量可以助推人向前跨过千山万水，南朝宋的宗悫年少时被问及志向时回答“愿乘长风破万里浪”。破万里浪的愿景足够振奋人心，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">但真正能让普通人战胜巨浪的关键因素还是拥有强大助推力的风。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">诗仙李白以浪漫飘逸著称，在他的想象国度中，大鹏鸟能够“扶摇直上九万里”的前提是“同风起”，凭借风力飞到上九天云外，然后在“风歇时下来”。即便是大鹏这样传说中的神鸟，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">也需要静候风起，借势而行。</span></p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（中国-云南-崇圣寺-大鹏金翅鸟广场）</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：WaitforLigh / 图虫创意）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.7342593\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"png\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_png/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSZvBqo9a6yJZEUOXiaSRPdf6vpH6jl6OqTjIKrzV0Ie2xY6V6spdc0bQ/640?wx_fmt=png\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">曹雪芹在《红楼梦》中借薛宝钗之口吐露出“韶华休笑本无根，好风凭借力，送我上青云”的佳句。<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">本该腐烂在尘埃里的柳絮在风的借力之下，也可以青云直上。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">受文学修辞的影响，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">在我们的语言里风渐渐从一种自然现象，变成了一种无形推力的代名词。</span>人们用风来指代大环境的变化趋势，用“风口”来指代机遇。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">“借东风”、“一帆风顺”都是吉祥话儿</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：saintho / 图虫创意）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.7407407\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"jpeg\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/DCftNYRGoKVfxMxuX4Bc0gJ7EX01kdUSzmCYCIpzjsrL1CF6ScUnibtGMN22T0zmMbEJgaiardenk3q5z5RsibHaw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">网络时代随着信息传播速度的加快，造梗的速度也在提升，某些汉字或词汇的语义都获得了极大地丰富。“站在风口上，猪都会飞起来”的话得到了广泛传播与认同。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">人又何不是如此呢？所谓时势造英雄，每个人的成功都离不开个人的努力，但能到什么样的高度就需要看环境和机遇。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">有太多的例子已经证明，人生大多时候正确的选择大于盲目地努力，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">借助一阵好的风不仅能让人的奋斗事半功倍，也可以让自己的努力变得更有意义。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">在2020这个特殊的年份尤其是这样。今年受疫情影响，社会经济受到了一定的冲击，人们越来越多的谈论到经济的趋势，风向究竟会朝哪个方向变化。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"text-align: left;font-size: 12px;color: rgb(160, 160, 160);box-sizing: border-box;\"><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"font-size: 13px;box-sizing: border-box;\">城市熙熙攘攘，车水马龙，却很少有人能捕捉到正确的方向</span></p><p style=\"margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;font-size: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;\">（图片：gui yong nian / 图虫创意）</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: 1.8px;box-sizing: border-box;\">▼</span><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p></section></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;vertical-align: middle;display: inline-block;line-height: 0;width: 100%;border-width: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><img data-ratio=\"0.6675926\" data-w=\"1080\" style=\"vertical-align: middle; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; max-width: 600px\" width=\"100%\" data-type=\"png\" style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">危机伴随着机遇是老生常谈了，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">采取什么渠道获得信息才是更好的看风姿势，这是职场人真正关心的问题。</span></p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">工欲善其事，必先利其器。正如想要精确测量风向和风速就需要精确刻度的风向风速仪一样，掌握最新的行业职场动向也需要精确而专业的平台。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">省去冗杂环节提升效率，</span>直接看到你想看的。</p></section><section style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\" powered-by=\"xiumi.us\"><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"><br style=\"box-sizing: border-box;\"></p><p style=\"white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\">更有即时更新的海量信息帮你掌握最新的行业动向，<span style=\"color: rgb(110, 141, 156);box-sizing: border-box;\">手机下载BOSS直聘就相当于手上持有了一个风向标，</span>随时随地了解风向变化，助力职场人在浪潮汹涌的当下乘风破浪。</p></section><section style=\"margin: 6px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;\"
